<pr_description>
Inline nested embeddable generates wrong column name when parent is null
### Describe the bug

When a parent inline embeddable is set to `null`, nested embeddables fail to generate a correct column name.

We were trying to upgrade from 6.4.15 to 6.6.x and our tests started failing.

https://github.com/atachh/mikro-nested-embeddable-bug

      }

      if (prop.fieldNames) {
        Utils.renameKey(data, k, prop.fieldNames[0]);
      }
    });

    return data;
  }

  protected inlineEmbeddables<T extends object>(meta: EntityMetadata<T>, data: T, where?: boolean): void {
    /* v8 ignore next */
    if (data == null) {
      return;
    }

    Utils.keys(data).forEach(k => {
      if (Utils.isOperator(k as string)) {
        Utils.asArray(data[k]).forEach(payload => this.inlineEmbeddables(meta, payload as T, where));
      }
    });

    meta.props.forEach(prop => {
      if (prop.kind === ReferenceKind.EMBEDDED && prop.object && !where && Utils.isObject(data[prop.name])) {
        return;
      }

      if (prop.kind === ReferenceKind.EMBEDDED && Utils.isObject(data[prop.name])) {
        const props = prop.embeddedProps;
        let unknownProp = false;

        Object.keys(data[prop.name] as Dictionary).forEach(kk => {
          // explicitly allow `$exists`, `$eq`, `$ne` and `$elemMatch` operators here as they can't be misused this way
          const operator = Object.keys(data[prop.name] as Dictionary).some(
            f => Utils.isOperator(f) && !['$exists', '$ne', '$eq', '$elemMatch'].includes(f),
          );

          if (operator) {
            throw ValidationError.cannotUseOperatorsInsideEmbeddables(meta.class, prop.name, data);
          }

          if (prop.object && where) {
            const inline: (payload: any, sub: EntityProperty, path: string[]) => void = (
              payload: any,
              sub: EntityProperty,
              path: string[],
            ) => {
              if (sub.kind === ReferenceKind.EMBEDDED && Utils.isObject(payload[sub.embedded![1]])) {
                return Object.keys(payload[sub.embedded![1]]).forEach(kkk => {
                  if (!sub.embeddedProps[kkk]) {
                    throw ValidationError.invalidEmbeddableQuery(meta.class, kkk, sub.type);
                  }

                  inline(payload[sub.embedded![1]], sub.embeddedProps[kkk], [...path, sub.fieldNames[0]]);
                });
              }

              data[`${path.join('.')}.${sub.fieldNames[0]}` as EntityKey<T>] = payload[sub.embedded![1]];
            };

            const parentPropName = kk.substring(0, kk.indexOf('.'));

            // we might be using some native JSON operator, e.g. with mongodb's `$geoWithin` or `$exists`
            if (props[kk]) {
              /* v8 ignore next */
              inline(data[prop.name], props[kk] || props[parentPropName], [prop.fieldNames[0]]);
            } else if (props[parentPropName]) {
              data[`${prop.fieldNames[0]}.${kk}` as keyof T] = (data[prop.name] as Dictionary)[kk];
            } else {
              unknownProp = true;
            }
          } else if (props[kk]) {
            data[props[kk].fieldNames[0] as EntityKey<T>] = data[prop.name][
              props[kk].embedded![1] as never
            ] as T[EntityKey<T>];
    const padding = ' '.repeat(level * 2);
    const idx = this.#tmpIndex++;

    ret.push(`${padding}if (Array.isArray(entity${entityKey})) {`);
    ret.push(`${padding}  ret${dataKey} = [];`);
    ret.push(`${padding}  entity${entityKey}.forEach((_, idx_${idx}) => {`);
    ret.push(
      this.getEmbeddedPropertySnapshot(
        meta,
        prop,
        context,
        level + 2,
        [...path, `[idx_${idx}]`],
        `${dataKey}[idx_${idx}]`,
        true,
      ),
    );
    ret.push(`${padding}  });`);

    if (this.shouldSerialize(prop, dataKey)) {
      ret.push(`${padding}  ret${dataKey} = cloneEmbeddable(ret${dataKey});`);
    }

    ret.push(`${padding}}`);

    return ret.join('\n');
  }

  /**
   * we need to serialize only object embeddables, and only the top level ones, so root object embeddable
   * properties and first child nested object embeddables with inlined parent
   */
  private shouldSerialize(prop: EntityProperty, dataKey: string): boolean {
    dataKey = dataKey.replace(/^\./, '');
    const contains = (str: string, re: RegExp) => (str.match(re) || []).length > 0;
    const a = contains(dataKey, /\./g);
    const b = contains(dataKey, /\[idx_/g);

    return !!prop.object && !a && !b;
  }

  private getEmbeddedPropertySnapshot<T>(
    meta: EntityMetadata<T>,
    prop: EntityProperty<T>,
    context: Map<string, any>,
    level: number,
    path: string[],
    dataKey: string,
    object = prop.object,
  ): string {
    const padding = ' '.repeat(level * 2);
    const nullCond = `entity${path.map(k => this.wrap(k)).join('')} === null`;
    let ret = level === 1 ? '' : '\n';

    if (object) {
      ret += `${padding}if (${nullCond}) ret${dataKey} = null;\n`;
    } else {
      ret += `${padding}if (${nullCond}) {\n`;
      ret +=
        meta.props
          .filter(
            p =>
              p.embedded?.[0] === prop.name &&
              // object for JSON embeddable
              (p.object || p.persist !== false),
          )
          .map(childProp => {
            const childDataKey =
              meta.embeddable || prop.object ? dataKey + this.wrap(childProp.embedded![1]) : this.wrap(childProp.name);
            return `${padding}  ret${childDataKey} = null;`;
          })
          .join('\n') + `\n`;
      ret += `${padding}}\n`;
    }

    const cond = `entity${path.map(k => this.wrap(k)).join('')} != null`;
    ret += `${padding}if (${cond}) {\n`;

    if (object) {
      ret += `${padding}  ret${dataKey} = {};\n`;
    }

   740	  private registerCustomType<T>(prop: EntityProperty<T>, context: Map<string, any>) {
   741	    const convertorKey = this.safeKey(prop.name);
   742	    context.set(`convertToDatabaseValue_${convertorKey}`, (val: any) => {

   749	    });

cat > /testbed/temp/repro.ts <<'EOF'
import { EntitySchema, MikroORM } from '@mikro-orm/sqlite';

class Nested { value!: string; }
class ParentEmb { nested!: Nested; other!: string; }
class Root { id!: number; parent?: ParentEmb | null; }

const NestedSchema = new EntitySchema<Nested>({
  class: Nested,
  embeddable: true,
  properties: {
    value: { type: 'string', nullable: true },
  },
});

const ParentEmbSchema = new EntitySchema<ParentEmb>({
  class: ParentEmb,
  embeddable: true,
  properties: {
    nested: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => Nested, nullable: true },
    other: { type: 'string', nullable: true },
  },
});

const RootSchema = new EntitySchema<Root>({
  class: Root,
  tableName: 'root',
  properties: {
    id: { type: 'number', primary: true },
    parent: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => ParentEmb, nullable: true },
  },
});

const orm = await MikroORM.init({
  entities: [RootSchema, ParentEmbSchema, NestedSchema],
  dbName: ':memory:',
  debug: ['query'],
});

console.log(await orm.schema.getCreateSchemaSQL({ wrap: false }));
await orm.schema.createSchema();
const r = orm.em.create(Root, { id: 1, parent: null });
await orm.em.persistAndFlush(r);
console.log('inserted');
await orm.close(true);
EOF

import type {
  Dictionary,
  EntityData,
  EntityDictionary,
  EntityKey,
  EntityMetadata,
  EntityName,
  EntityProperty,
  IMetadataStorage,
  Primary,
} from '../typings.js';

  compareArrays,
  compareBooleans,
  compareBuffers,
  compareObjects,
  equals,
  parseJsonSafe,
  Utils,
} from './Utils.js';

import { EntityIdentifier } from '../entity/EntityIdentifier.js';
import type { Configuration } from './Configuration.js';
import { PolymorphicRef } from '../entity/PolymorphicRef.js';

type Comparator<T> = (a: T, b: T, options?: { includeInverseSides?: boolean }) => EntityData<T>;
type ResultMapper<T> = (result: EntityData<T>) => EntityData<T> | null;
type SnapshotGenerator<T> = (entity: T) => EntityData<T>;
type PkGetter<T> = (entity: T) => Primary<T>;
type PkSerializer<T> = (entity: T) => string;
type CompositeKeyPart = string | CompositeKeyPart[];

/** @internal Generates and caches JIT-compiled functions for comparing, snapshotting, and mapping entity data. */
export class EntityComparator {
  readonly #comparators = new Map<EntityMetadata, Comparator<any>>();
  readonly #mappers = new Map<EntityMetadata, ResultMapper<any>>();
  readonly #snapshotGenerators = new Map<EntityMetadata, SnapshotGenerator<any>>();
  readonly #pkGetters = new Map<EntityMetadata, PkGetter<any>>();
  readonly #pkGettersConverted = new Map<EntityMetadata, PkGetter<any>>();
  readonly #pkSerializers = new Map<EntityMetadata, PkSerializer<any>>();
  #tmpIndex = 0;
  readonly #metadata: IMetadataStorage;
  readonly #platform: Platform;
  readonly #config?: Configuration;

  constructor(metadata: IMetadataStorage, platform: Platform, config?: Configuration) {
    this.#metadata = metadata;
    this.#platform = platform;
    this.#config = config;
  }

  /**
   * Computes difference between two entities.
   */
  diffEntities<T extends object>(
    entityName: EntityName<T>,
    a: EntityData<T>,
    b: EntityData<T>,
    options?: { includeInverseSides?: boolean },
  ): EntityData<T> {
    const comparator = this.getEntityComparator(entityName);
    return Utils.callCompiledFunction(comparator, a as T, b as T, options);
  }

  /** Returns true if two entity snapshots are identical (no differences). */
  matching<T extends object>(entityName: EntityName<T>, a: EntityData<T>, b: EntityData<T>): boolean {
    const diff = this.diffEntities(entityName, a, b);
    return Utils.getObjectKeysSize(diff) === 0;
  }

  /**
   * Removes ORM specific code from entities and prepares it for serializing. Used before change set computation.
   * References will be mapped to primary keys, collections to arrays of primary keys.
   */
  prepareEntity<T extends object>(entity: T): EntityData<T> {
    const generator = this.getSnapshotGenerator<T>(entity.constructor);
    return Utils.callCompiledFunction(generator, entity);
  }

  /**
   * Maps database columns to properties.
   */
  mapResult<T>(meta: EntityMetadata<T>, result: EntityDictionary<T>): EntityData<T> {
    const mapper = this.getResultMapper<T>(meta);
    return Utils.callCompiledFunction(mapper, result)!;
  }

  /**
   * @internal Highly performance-sensitive method.
   */
  getPkGetter<T>(meta: EntityMetadata<T>): PkGetter<T> {
    const exists = this.#pkGetters.get(meta);

    /* v8 ignore next */
    if (exists) {
      return exists;
    }

    const lines: string[] = [];
    const context = new Map<string, any>();
    context.set('isEntityOrRef', (val: any) => Utils.isEntity(val, true));

    if (meta.primaryKeys.length > 1) {
      lines.push(`  const cond = {`);
      meta.primaryKeys.forEach(pk => {
        if (meta.properties[pk].kind !== ReferenceKind.SCALAR) {
          lines.push(
            `    ${pk}: (entity${this.wrap(pk)} != null && isEntityOrRef(entity${this.wrap(pk)})) ? entity${this.wrap(pk)}.__helper.getPrimaryKey() : entity${this.wrap(pk)},`,
          );
        } else {
          lines.push(`    ${pk}: entity${this.wrap(pk)},`);
        }
      });
      lines.push(`  };`);
      lines.push(`  if (${meta.primaryKeys.map(pk => `cond.${pk} == null`).join(' || ')}) return null;`);
      lines.push(`  return cond;`);

function(entity) {
  const ret = {};
  if (typeof entity.id !== 'undefined') {
    ret.id = entity.id;
  }

  if (entity.parent === null) {
    ret.parent_nested = null;
    ret.parent_other = null;
  }
  if (entity.parent != null) {

    if (entity.parent.nested === null) {
      ret.parent_nested_value = null;
    }
    if (entity.parent.nested != null) {
      if (typeof entity.parent.nested.value !== 'undefined') ret.parent_nested_value = clone(entity.parent.nested.value);
    }

    if (typeof entity.parent.other !== 'undefined') ret.parent_other = clone(entity.parent.other);
  }

  return ret;
}

        }

        return [childProp];
      });
    };

    const getChildDataKey = (childProp: EntityProperty): string => {
      if (!meta.embeddable && !prop.object) {
        return this.wrap(childProp.name);
      }

      const path: string[] = [];
      let tmp = childProp;

      while (tmp.embedded && tmp.embedded[0] !== prop.name) {
        path.unshift(tmp.embedded[1]);
        tmp = meta.properties[tmp.embedded[0]];
      }

      path.unshift(tmp.embedded![1]);

      return dataKey + path.map(k => this.wrap(k)).join('"'"''"'"');
    };

    if (object) {
      ret += `${padding}if (${nullCond}) ret${dataKey} = null;\n`;
    } else {
      ret += `${padding}if (${nullCond}) {\n`;
      ret +=
        getNullProps(prop)
          .map(childProp => {
            return `${padding}  ret${getChildDataKey(childProp)} = null;`;
          })
          .join('"'"'\n'"'"') + `\n`;
      ret += `${padding}}\n`;
    }
'

import { EntitySchema, MikroORM } from '@mikro-orm/sqlite';
class Nested { value; }
class ParentEmb { nested; other; }
class Root { id; parent; }
const NestedSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Nested, embeddable: true, properties: { value: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const ParentEmbSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: ParentEmb, embeddable: true, properties: { nested: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => Nested, nullable: true }, other: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const RootSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Root, tableName: 'root', properties: { id: { type: 'number', primary: true }, parent: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => ParentEmb, nullable: true } } });
const orm = await MikroORM.init({ entities: [RootSchema, ParentEmbSchema, NestedSchema], dbName: ':memory:', allowGlobalContext: true });
await orm.schema.create();
const r = orm.em.create(Root, { id: 1, parent: null });
orm.em.persist(r);
await orm.em.flush();
const rows = await orm.em.getConnection().execute('select * from root');
console.log(rows);
await orm.close(true);
EOF

   591	  private resolveTPTIdentifiers<T extends object>(changeSet: ChangeSet<T>): void {
   592	    if (changeSet.meta.inheritanceType !== 'tpt' || !changeSet.meta.tptParent) {
   593	      return;

   647	   * We do need to map to the change set payload too, as it will be used in the originalEntityData for new entities.
   648	   */
   649	  mapReturnedValues<T extends object>(
   650	    entity: T | null | undefined,
   651	    payload: EntityDictionary<T>,
   652	    row: Dictionary | undefined,
   653	    meta: EntityMetadata<T>,
   654	    upsert = false,

import { EntitySchema, MikroORM } from '@mikro-orm/sqlite';
class Nested { value; }
class ParentEmb { nested; other; }
class Root { id; parent; }
const NestedSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Nested, embeddable: true, properties: { value: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const ParentEmbSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: ParentEmb, embeddable: true, properties: { nested: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => Nested, nullable: true }, other: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const RootSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Root, tableName: 'root', properties: { id: { type: 'number', primary: true }, parent: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => ParentEmb, nullable: true } } });
const orm = await MikroORM.init({ entities: [RootSchema, ParentEmbSchema, NestedSchema], dbName: ':memory:', allowGlobalContext: true });
await orm.schema.create();
const r = orm.em.create(Root, { id: 1, parent: null });
orm.em.persist(r);
await orm.em.flush();
const rows = await orm.em.getConnection().execute('select * from root');
console.log(rows);
const gen = orm.em.getComparator().getSnapshotGenerator(ParentEmb);
console.log(gen(Object.assign(new ParentEmb(), { nested: null, other: 'x' })));
await orm.close(true);

import { EntitySchema, MikroORM } from '@mikro-orm/sqlite';
class Leaf { value; }
class Mid { leaf; }
class ParentEmb { mid; other; }
class Root { id; parent; }
const LeafSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Leaf, embeddable: true, properties: { value: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const MidSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Mid, embeddable: true, properties: { leaf: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => Leaf, nullable: true } } });
const ParentEmbSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: ParentEmb, embeddable: true, properties: { mid: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => Mid, nullable: true }, other: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const RootSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Root, tableName: 'root', properties: { id: { type: 'number', primary: true }, parent: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => ParentEmb, nullable: true } } });
const orm = await MikroORM.init({ entities: [RootSchema, ParentEmbSchema, MidSchema, LeafSchema], dbName: ':memory:', allowGlobalContext: true });
console.log(await orm.schema.getCreateSchemaSQL({ wrap: false }));
await orm.schema.create();
const r = orm.em.create(Root, { id: 1, parent: null });
orm.em.persist(r);
await orm.em.flush();
console.log(await orm.em.getConnection().execute('select * from root'));
await orm.close(true);

cd /testbed && node --import=tsx - <<'EOF'
import { EntitySchema, MikroORM } from '@mikro-orm/sqlite';
class Nested { value; }
class ParentEmb { nested; other; }
class Root { id; parent; }
const NestedSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Nested, embeddable: true, properties: { value: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const ParentEmbSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: ParentEmb, embeddable: true, properties: { nested: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => Nested, nullable: true }, other: { type: 'string', nullable: true } } });
const RootSchema = new EntitySchema({ class: Root, tableName: 'root', properties: { id: { type: 'number', primary: true }, parent: { kind: 'embedded', entity: () => ParentEmb, nullable: true } } });
const orm = await MikroORM.init({ entities: [RootSchema, ParentEmbSchema, NestedSchema], dbName: ':memory:', allowGlobalContext: true });
await orm.schema.create();
const r = orm.em.create(Root, { id: 1, parent: { nested: { value: 'a' }, other: 'b' } });
orm.em.persist(r);
await orm.em.flush();
r.parent = null;
await orm.em.flush();
console.log(await orm.em.getConnection().execute('select * from root'));
await orm.close(true);
EOF
